===== --version =====
2.0.0

===== --help =====
Usage: ai-dev [options] [command]

AI development workflow CLI toolkit

Options:
  -V, --version                     output the version number
  --lang <locale>                   Output language (en|zh-TW)
  -h, --help                        display help for command

Commands:
  install [options]                 Install AI development environment
  update [options]                  Update packages and repositories
  clone [options]                   Distribute resources to configured AI tool
                                    directories
  status [options]                  Check environment status
  list [options]                    List installed resources
  toggle [options]                  Enable or disable installed resources
  add-repo [options] <repo>         Add and optionally clone a tracked
                                    repository
  add-custom-repo [options] <repo>  Add custom repository to
                                    ~/.config/ai-dev/repos.yaml
  update-custom-repo [options]      Update all custom repositories
  test [options] [path]             Run Bun tests
  coverage [options] [path]         Run tests with coverage
  derive-tests <path>               Read spec markdown files for test derivation
  project                           Project template and standards operations
  standards                         Manage standards profiles
  hooks                             Manage ECC hooks plugin
  sync                              Manage cross-device sync
  mem                               Manage claude-mem sync
  tui                               Launch interactive TUI
  help [command]                    display help for command

===== install --help =====
Usage: ai-dev install [options]

Install AI development environment

Options:
  --skip-npm      Skip global NPM package installation
  --skip-bun      Skip Bun package installation
  --skip-repos    Skip repository cloning
  --skip-skills   Skip skill distribution
  --sync-project  Sync project template files
  --json          Output result as JSON
  -h, --help      display help for command

===== update --help =====
Usage: ai-dev update [options]

Update packages and repositories

Options:
  --skip-npm      Skip global NPM package updates
  --skip-bun      Skip Bun package updates
  --skip-repos    Skip repository updates
  --skip-plugins  Skip plugin marketplace update
  --json          Output result as JSON
  -h, --help      display help for command

===== clone --help =====
Usage: ai-dev clone [options]

Distribute resources to configured AI tool directories

Options:
  --force            Overwrite existing conflicting files
  --skip-conflicts   Skip conflicting files
  --backup           Backup conflicting files before overwrite
  --sync-project     Also sync project-template files
  --no-sync-project  Skip project-template synchronization
  --json             Output result as JSON
  -h, --help         display help for command

===== list --help =====
Usage: ai-dev list [options]

List installed resources

Options:
  --target <target>  Target platform
  --type <type>      Resource type: skills|commands|agents|workflows
  --hide-disabled    Hide disabled resources
  --json             Output as JSON
  -h, --help         display help for command

===== toggle --help =====
Usage: ai-dev toggle [options]

Enable or disable installed resources

Options:
  --target <target>  Target platform
  --type <type>      Resource type
  --name <name>      Resource name
  --enable           Enable resource
  --disable          Disable resource
  --list             List resource toggle state
  -h, --help         display help for command

===== add-repo --help =====
Usage: ai-dev add-repo [options] <repo>

Add and optionally clone a tracked repository

Arguments:
  repo               GitHub repo (owner/name) or URL

Options:
  --name <name>      Custom repo name
  --branch <branch>  Tracked branch (default: "main")
  --skip-clone       Skip cloning and only register config
  --analyze          Analyze repository structure and suggest approach
  -h, --help         display help for command

===== add-custom-repo --help =====
Usage: ai-dev add-custom-repo [options] <repo>

Add custom repository to ~/.config/ai-dev/repos.yaml

Arguments:
  repo               GitHub repo (owner/name) or URL

Options:
  --name <name>      Custom repo name
  --branch <branch>  Tracked branch (default: "main")
  --no-clone         Do not clone repository before registering
  --fix              Create missing standard directories
  -h, --help         display help for command

===== update-custom-repo --help =====
Usage: ai-dev update-custom-repo [options]

Update all custom repositories

Options:
  --json      Output as JSON
  -h, --help  display help for command

===== test --help =====
Usage: ai-dev test [options] [path]

Run Bun tests

Arguments:
  path                     Optional test path

Options:
  -v, --verbose            Verbose output
  -x, --fail-fast          Stop on first failure
  -k, --keyword <keyword>  Filter tests by name
  --framework <framework>  Test framework (bun|npm|pytest|phpunit)
  --source <path>          Source path for framework-specific options
  -h, --help               display help for command

===== coverage --help =====
Usage: ai-dev coverage [options] [path]

Run tests with coverage

Arguments:
  path                     Optional test path

Options:
  --framework <framework>  Test framework (bun|npm|pytest|phpunit)
  --source <path>          Coverage source path
  -h, --help               display help for command

===== derive-tests --help =====
Usage: ai-dev derive-tests [options] <path>

Read spec markdown files for test derivation

Arguments:
  path        Spec file or directory

Options:
  -h, --help  display help for command

===== project --help =====
Usage: ai-dev project [options] [command]

Project template and standards operations

Options:
  -h, --help               display help for command

Commands:
  init [options] [target]  Initialize project from template
  update [options]         Run project update commands
  help [command]           display help for command

===== project init --help =====
Usage: ai-dev project init [options] [target]

Initialize project from template

Arguments:
  target      Target directory

Options:
  --force     Force overwrite existing files
  --json      Output as JSON
  -h, --help  display help for command

===== project update --help =====
Usage: ai-dev project update [options]

Run project update commands

Options:
  --only <tool>  Only run one tool (openspec|uds)
  --json         Output as JSON
  -h, --help     display help for command

===== standards --help =====
Usage: ai-dev standards [options] [command]

Manage standards profiles

Options:
  -h, --help                  display help for command

Commands:
  status [options]            Show current standards status
  list [options]              List available profiles
  switch [options] <profile>  Switch active profile
  show [options] <profile>    Show profile content
  overlaps [options]          Show overlapping definitions across profiles
  sync [options]              Sync standards state to .disabled directory
  help [command]              display help for command

  uninstall [options]  Uninstall hooks plugin

  help [command]       display help for command

===== sync --help =====
Usage: ai-dev sync [options] [command]

Manage cross-device sync

Options:
  -h, --help               display help for command

Commands:
  init [options]           Initialize sync config
  push [options]           Push local sync directories into repo dir
  pull [options]           Pull from repo dir into local directories
  status [options]         Show sync status
  add [options] <path>     Add a directory to sync
  remove [options] <path>  Remove directory from sync
  help [command]           display help for command

===== sync status =====
Sync status
- Initialized: true
- Repo: /home/valor/.config/ai-dev/sync-repo
- Local changes: 0
- Remote behind: 0
- Tracked directories: 1

===== sync push --help =====
Usage: ai-dev sync push [options]

Push local sync directories into repo dir

Options:
  --force     Force push to remote
  --json      Output as JSON
  -h, --help  display help for command

===== sync pull --help =====
Usage: ai-dev sync pull [options]

Pull from repo dir into local directories

Options:
  --no-delete  Keep local extra files
  --force      Overwrite local changes without prompt
  --json       Output as JSON
  -h, --help   display help for command

===== mem --help =====
Usage: ai-dev mem [options] [command]

Manage claude-mem sync

Options:
  -h, --help          display help for command

Commands:
  register [options]  Register this device to sync server
  push [options]      Push local data to sync server
  pull [options]      Pull remote data from sync server
  status [options]    Show mem sync status
  reindex [options]   Reindex local observations (auto-cleans duplicates)
  cleanup [options]   Remove duplicate observations from local database
  auto [options]      Configure automatic memory sync
  help [command]      display help for command

===== mem status =====
Memory sync status
- Device: (unregistered)
- Local observations: 0
- Pending push: 0
- Remote status: unavailable

===== mem auto --help =====
Usage: ai-dev mem auto [options]

Configure automatic memory sync

Options:
  --enable              Enable automatic sync
  --disable             Disable automatic sync
  --status              Show auto-sync status
  --interval <minutes>  Auto-sync interval in minutes
  --json                Output as JSON
  -h, --help            display help for command
